UKR_provide_smolguns_ai = {

		original_tag = UKR
	}

	visible = {
		UKR = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		is_ai = yes
		UKR = { has_war_with = RUS }
	}

		factor = 400

	UKR_hold_brovary = {
		icon = generic_civil_support
		allowed = {
			original_tag = UKR
		}
		#Fail trigger
		available = {
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 87
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 20
		fire_only_once = yes
		is_good = yes
		activation = {
			has_war = yes
			has_civil_war = no
			87 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					any_neighbor_state = {
						CONTROLLER = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
						OWNER = {
							tag = ROOT
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#Success
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_hold_brovary: timeout_effect"
			add_stability = 0.03
			add_war_support = 0.03
			87 = {
				save_event_target_as = state
			}
			#.5 #replace with the relevant event
		}
		#Fail
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_hold_brovary: complete_effect"
			87 = {
				save_event_target_as = state
			}
			#.6 #replace with the relevant event
		}
	}

UKR_information_war = {
    UKR_psychological_operation_bet = {
		icon = UKR_discrediting_Russia
		fire_only_once = no
		cost = 40
		available = {
			tag = UKR
		}
		visible = {
			tag = UKR
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_psychological_operation
			}
			has_completed_focus = Information_war
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision UKR_psychological_operation_bet"
		    custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_psychological_operation_cet
		    hidden_effect = {
			    if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = UKR_foreign_journalism
					}
					add_to_variable = { var = UKR_monthly_increase_var_add value = -2.5 }
					clear_variable = UKR_inf_war_making_bet_political_power_factor
					clear_variable = UKR_inf_war_making_bet_war_support_weekly_factor
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = UKR_military_personnel
					}
					clear_variable = UKR_inf_war_making_bet_war_support_factor
					clear_variable = UKR_inf_war_making_bet_weekly_manpower
					clear_variable = UKR_inf_war_making_bet_command_power_gain_mult
				}
			    clr_country_flag = UKR_foreign_journalism
				clr_country_flag = UKR_military_personnel
				set_country_flag = UKR_psychological_operation
				add_to_variable = {
					var = UKR_monthly_increase_var_add
					value = 1.5
				}
				RUS = { 
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = UKR_propaganda_debuff }
					set_variable = { var = UKR_propaganda_debuff_political_power_factor value = -0.1 }
				}
			}
		}	
	}
